<div class="hp_desc_main_content ">
<span data-et-view="adUAVGPZPPESHbfALbLEDSGeFTYcUO:2" style="position:absolute;width:1px;height:1px;opacity:1;"></span>
<div id="summary" class="">
<div class="chain-content chain-content-break-line">
<h3 class="hp_header_compact hp-hotel-description-header">
Stay in the Heart of Cincinnati
<span class="city_centre_map_link">
–
<a data-source="heart_link" class="show_map city_centre_map_link_show_map " href="javascript:void(0);" data-central-polygon="39.10628112028938,-84.51912397518754,39.10562341592585,-84.51905960217118,39.10538197860695,-84.52051872387528,39.10446617436265,-84.52032560482621,39.09314121973792,-84.5175788551569,39.09480657699581,-84.50963951647282,39.096505200881445,-84.50474716722965,39.1008015374713,-84.49732281267643,39.104464873495864,-84.50341679155827,39.10779501377678,-84.50813747942448,39.10628112028938,-84.51912397518754" data-coords="," rel="" id="with-city-centre-polygon" data-map-id="with-city-centre-polygon">
Excellent location – show map
</a>
</span>
</h3>
</div>
<p><span class="hp-description--property-name-top-ranked dtri"><i class="bicon-acstar"></i>One of our top picks in Cincinnati.</span>Located just a short distance from <span class="hp-social_proof-item-featured-topic jq_tooltip hp-social_proof-item-featured-topic-element" data-component="tooltip" data-et-view="TAeKPWbOTBYfQfQAYbQTZOUdTSaTfRe:1" data-et-mouseenter="TAeKPWbOTBYfQfQAYbQTZOUdTSaTfRe:2" data-tooltip-text="8 review highlights from guests">Fountain Square</span>, this Cincinnati hotel offers Wi-Fi and rooms equipped with a flat-screen TV, sitting area, and work desk. The <span class="hp-social_proof-item-featured-topic jq_tooltip hp-social_proof-item-featured-topic-element" data-component="tooltip" data-et-view="TAeKPWbOTBYfQfQAYbQTZOUdTSaTfRe:1" data-et-mouseenter="TAeKPWbOTBYfQfQAYbQTZOUdTSaTfRe:2" data-tooltip-text="23 review highlights from guests">Great</span> American Ball Park is half a mile away.</p>
<p>Floor-to-ceiling windows along with plush bedding are featured in each modern room at the Cincinnati Westin. Tea and coffee-making facilities along with an in-room electronic safe are also included.</p>
<p>Continental breakfast is served each morning and it features hot coffee or tea along with fresh fruit and pastries. McCormick &amp; Schmick’s Seafood Restaurant serves lunch and dinner.</p>
<p>Guests can swim in the indoor pool or use the business center that offers fax and photocopying services.</p>
<p>Plenty of shopping and dining are located within <span data-et-mouseenter="TAeKPWbOTBYfQfQAYbQTZOUdTSaTfRe:2" data-et-view="TAeKPWbOTBYfQfQAYbQTZOUdTSaTfRe:1" data-tooltip-text="5 review highlights from guests" data-component="tooltip" class="hp-social_proof-item-featured-topic jq_tooltip hp-social_proof-item-featured-topic-element">walking distance</span> of the Westin Cincinnati. The National Underground Railroad Freedom Center is half a mile away. 
<br></p>
</div>
<p class="hp-desc-review-highlight">
This property also has one of the top-rated locations in Cincinnati! Guests are happier about it compared to other properties in the area.
</p>
<p class="hp-desc-review-highlight hp-desc-traveller-type--ph-v0">
Couples in particular like the location – they rated it <strong>9.1</strong> for a two-person trip.
</p>
<p class="hp-desc-we-speak">
We speak your language!
</p>
<p class="summary  hotel_meta_style">
<span class="hp-desc-highlighted">
The Westin Cincinnati has been welcoming Booking.com guests since Apr 24, 2012<br>
</span>
Hotel Chain:
Westin
</p>

<h3 class="hp-description-sub-header" data-et-view="">
Most Popular Facilities

<div class="hp-section-container hp-hotelier-info-block">
<div class="hp-section-header">
An Inside Look at The Westin Cincinnati
</div>
<div class="hp-section">
<div class="hotelier-info">
<p>Each of our 456 contemporary, oversized guestrooms
and suites offer striking views of the city skyline or
historic Fountain Square and feature our Heavenly
Bed* and Heavenly Bath*, floor-to-ceiling windows,
wireless and wired internet, and two telephones, one
cordless with speaker capabilities. Other amenities
include a work station with ergonomic leather chair,
in-room coolers, electronic safes and coffeemakers.
Westin also offers guests a 100% smoke-free facility. Let us take care of you with services like concierge, business center, gift shop, 24 hour in-room dining, valet
and self-parking. Energize with our 24-hour WestinWORKOUT® Fitness Studio featuring treadmills, stationary bicycles,elliptical and free weights. Each machine has a personal TV and iPod dock. Located next to the gym, our sunlit pool area includes an indoor heated lap pool and
whirlpool. Enjoy the following on-site restaurants: Ingredients
provides gourmet grab-and-go café options; McCormick
&amp; Schmick’s Seafood Restaurant offers lunch weekdays
and dinner nightly, featuring an impressive array of
fresh seafood, plus steak, salads and pasta. Over Vine
Bar is the perfect place to catch up and unwind.</p>
</div>
</div>
<div style="height:15px"></div>
</div>

</span>
<span>Children and Extra Beds</span>
</p>
<p>All children are welcome.</p>
<p class="positive_policy_free
contains_free_row">
<span class="hp-free-facility-row free-policy-border">
<strong>Free!</strong>
Up to two children under 17 years stay free of charge when using existing beds.
</span> <br>
</p>
<p>Up to two additional older children or adults are charged USD 20 per person per night when using existing beds.</p>
<p class="positive_policy_free
contains_free_row">
<span class="hp-free-facility-row free-policy-border">
<strong>Free!</strong>
One older child or adult stays free of charge in an extra bed.
</span> <br>
</p>
<p class="positive_policy_free
contains_free_row">
<span class="hp-free-facility-row free-policy-border">
<strong>Free!</strong>
One child under 4 years stays free of charge in a crib.
</span> <br>
</p>
<p>The maximum number of extra beds/cribs in a room is 1.</p>
<p style="">Any type of extra bed or crib is upon request and needs to be confirmed by management.</p>
<p>Additional fees are not calculated automatically in the total cost and will have to be paid for separately during your stay.</p>

<div class=" review-policy reviews-new-title--fix-top clearfix review-policy-fix ">
<i class="review-policy__icon">눱</i>
<div class="review-policy__header-group">
<h2 class="review-policy__header">
100% Verified Reviews
</h2>
<h3 class="review-policy__subheader">
Real guests. Real stays. Real opinions.
<a class="review-policy__open" data-component="core/lightbox/trigger" href="#guidelines_content">Read more</a>
</h3>
</div>
<style>
.guidelines_content {
background: #fff;
padding: 12px 24px;
text-align: justify;
color: #003580;
}
.guidelines_content_lightbox {
background: #fff;
padding: 12px 24px;
text-align: justify;
height: 400px;
overflow-y: scroll;
color: #003580;
}
.guidelines_content p,
.guidelines_content_lightbox p {
margin: 1em 0;
}
.guidelines_content .head,
.guidelines_content_lightbox .head {
font-weight: bold;
font-size: 16px;
}

.guidelines_content {
width: auto;
text-align: left;
}
}
.lang_is_rtl .guidelines_content{
direction: rtl;
text-align: right;
}
</style>
<div id="guidelines_content" class="guidelines_content_lightbox" style="display:none;">
<p class="headline">Booking.com Guest Review Guidelines</p>
<i>To keep the rating score and review content relevant for your upcoming trip, we archive reviews older than 24 months.</i>
<p>Only a customer who has booked through Booking.com and stayed at the property in question can write a review. This allows us to verify that our reviews come from real guests like you. Who better to tell others about the free breakfast, friendly staff, or their comfortable room than someone who’s stayed at the property?</p>
<p>We want you to share your story, with both the good and the not-so-good. All we ask is that you follow a few simple guidelines.</p>
<p class="head"><strong>Reviews Vision</strong></p>
<p>We believe review contributions and property responses will highlight a wide range of opinions and experiences, which is critical in helping guests make informed decisions about where to stay.</p>
<p class="head"><strong>Reviews Principles</strong></p>
<p>Contributions to Booking.com are a reflection of the dedication of our guests and properties, so we treat them with the utmost respect.</p>
<p>Whether negative or positive, we'll post every comment in full, as quickly as possible, after it's moderated to comply with Booking.com guidelines. We'll also provide transparency over the status of submitted content.</p>
<p>After a review has been submitted, you can modify it by contacting Booking.com customer service.</p>
<p>We'll use the same guidelines and standards for all user-generated content, and for the property responses to that content.</p>
<p>We'll allow the contributions to speak for themselves, and we won’t be the judge of reality. Booking.com’s role is to be a feedback distributor for both guests and properties.</p>
<p class="head"><strong>Guidelines and Standards for Reviews</strong></p>
<p>These guidelines and standards aim to keep the content on Booking.com relevant and family-friendly, without limiting expression or strong opinions. They're also applicable regardless of the comment's tone. </p>
<p><strong>Contributions should be travel related.</strong> The most helpful contributions are detailed and help others make better decisions. Please don’t include personal, political, ethical, or religious commentary. Promotional content will be removed and issues concerning Booking.com’s services should be routed to our Customer Service or Accommodation Service teams.</p>
<p><strong>Contributions should be appropriate for a global audience.</strong> Please avoid using profanity or attempts to approximate profanity with creative spelling, in any language. Comments and media that include hate speech, discriminatory remarks, threats, sexually explicit remarks, violence, or the promotion of illegal activity are not permitted. </p>
<p><strong>All content should be genuine and unique to the guest.</strong> Reviews are most valuable when they are original and unbiased. Your contribution should be yours. Booking.com property partners should not post on behalf of guests or offer incentives in exchange for reviews. Attempts to bring down the rating of a competitor by submitting a negative review will not be tolerated.</p>
<p><strong>Respect the privacy of others.</strong> Booking.com will make an effort to obscure email addresses, telephone numbers, website addresses, social media accounts, and other similar details.</p>
<p><strong>The opinions expressed in contributions are those of Booking.com customers and properties, and not of Booking.com. Booking.com does not accept responsibility or liability for any reviews or responses. Booking.com is a distributor (without any obligation to verify) and not a publisher of these comments and responses.</strong></p>
<p>By default, reviews are sorted based on the date of the review and on additional criteria to display the most relevant reviews, including but not limited to: your language, reviews with text, and non-anonymous reviews. Additional sorting options might be available (by type of traveler, by score, etc...).</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="revc_write_a_review_login_intro" style="display:none;">
<h3>Verified reviews from real guests.</h3><p>We have more than 70 million property reviews, and they're all from <strong>real, verified guests.</strong>
</p><div class="rlp-intro">
<div class="rlp-intro__container clearfix">
<h3 class="rlp-intro__title">How does it work?</h3>
<ul class="rlp-intro-how">
<li class="rlp-intro-how__item fl">
<div class="rlp-intro-how__container rlp-intro-how__container--tickfull">
<div class="rlp-intro-how__sub-container">
<p class="rlp-intro-how__num rlp-intro-how__num--tickfull">1</p>
<p class="rlp-intro-how__icon bicon-tickfull"></p>
</div>
</div>
<h4 class="rlp-intro-how__title">It starts with a booking</h4>
<p class="rlp-intro-how__desc">The only way to leave a review is to first make a booking. That's how we know our reviews come from real guests who have stayed at the property.</p>
</li>
<li class="rlp-intro-how__arrow fl">
<p class="rlp-intro-how__arrow-icon bicon-rightchevron"></p>
</li>
<li class="rlp-intro-how__item fl">
<div class="rlp-intro-how__container rlp-intro-how__container--citytrip">
<div class="rlp-intro-how__sub-container">
<p class="rlp-intro-how__num rlp-intro-how__num--citytrip">2</p>
<p class="rlp-intro-how__icon bicon-citytrip"></p>
</div>
</div>
<h4 class="rlp-intro-how__title">Followed by a trip</h4>
<p class="rlp-intro-how__desc">When guests stay at the property, they check out how quiet the room is, how friendly the staff is, and more.</p>
</li>
<li class="rlp-intro-how__arrow fl">
<p class="rlp-intro-how__arrow-icon bicon-rightchevron"></p>
</li>
<li class="rlp-intro-how__item fl">
<div class="rlp-intro-how__container rlp-intro-how__container--feedback">
<div class="rlp-intro-how__sub-container">
<p class="rlp-intro-how__num rlp-intro-how__num--feedback">3</p>
<p class="rlp-intro-how__icon bicon-feedback"></p>
</div>
</div>
<h4 class="rlp-intro-how__title">And finally, a review</h4>
<p class="rlp-intro-how__desc">After their trip, guests tell us about their stay. We check for naughty words and verify the authenticity of all guest reviews before adding them to our site.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>
<p>If you booked through us and want to leave a review, please sign in first.</p>
<div class="intro_footer">
<a href="https://secure.booking.com/reviewtimeline.html" class="revc_write_a_review_login_button">Sign in and leave a review</a>
</div>
